###################################################################
# Triggered modifiers are here.
# these are checked for each countries once/month and then applied.
#
# Effects are fully scriptable here.
###################################################################

naval_oil_requirements_I = {
	potential = {
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 50 }
	}
	trigger = {
		total_amount_of_ships = 50
	}
	
	global_crude_oil = -0.05

	icon = 16
	
}

naval_oil_requirements_II = {
	potential = {
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 100 }
		total_amount_of_ships = 50
	}
	trigger = {
		total_amount_of_ships = 100
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 150 }
	}
	
	global_crude_oil = -0.1
	icon = 16
}

naval_oil_requirements_III = {
	potential = {
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 150 }
		total_amount_of_ships = 100
	}
	trigger = {
		total_amount_of_ships = 150
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 200 }
	}
	
	global_crude_oil = -0.15
	icon = 16
}

naval_oil_requirements_IV = {
	potential = {
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 200 }
		total_amount_of_ships = 150
	}
	trigger = {
		total_amount_of_ships = 200
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 250 }
	}
	
	global_crude_oil = -0.2
	icon = 16
}

naval_oil_requirements_V = {
	potential = {
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 250 }
		total_amount_of_ships = 200
	}
	trigger = {
		total_amount_of_ships = 250
		not = { total_amount_of_ships = 300 }
	}
	
	global_crude_oil = -0.2
	icon = 16
}

tungsten_amunition = {
	potential = {}
	trigger = {
		high_density_alloys = 2
		medium_velocity_gun	= 2

		or = {
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_SWE 
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_SPA 
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_SPR 
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_POR 
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_CAN 
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_CHI 
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_JAP 
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_tungsten_GER 
		
			8312 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			} 
			5753 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			} 
			4535 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			} 
			4347 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			} 
			101 = {
				or = {
					controller = { faction = this }
					controller = { vassal_of = this }
					controlled_by = this
				}
			} 
		}
	}
	
	hard_attack = 0.15
}

## Neutrality
neutrality = {

	potential = {
		not = {
			or = {
				faction = allies
				faction = axis
				faction = comintern
			}
			tag = USA
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		not = {
			or = {
				faction = allies
				faction = axis
				faction = comintern
				war = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	officer_recruitment = -0.25
	global_manpower_modifier = -0.25
	land_build_speed = 0.02
	tank_build_speed = 0.02
	air_build_speed = 0.02
	naval_build_speed = 0.02
	counter_espionage = 0.1
	
	icon = 14
}
## Winter War
winter_war = {

	potential = {
		not =  {has_global_flag = NO_MODIFIERS }
		tag = FIN
	}
	
	trigger = {
		tag = FIN
		not = {
			faction = axis
			faction = allies
		}
		FIN = {
			war_with = SOV
		}
		
	}
	
	org_regain = 0.025
	reinforcement_bonus = 0.25
	land_organisation = 0.025
	
	icon = 4
}

## Pact of Steel
pact_of_steel = {

	potential = {
		faction = axis
		not = { has_global_flag = tripartite_pact }
	}

	trigger = {
		GER = { faction = axis }
		ITA = { faction = axis }
	}
	
	global_supplies = 0.025
	research_efficiency = 0.025
	
	icon = 12
}
## Tripartite pact
tripartite_pact = {

	potential = {
		faction = axis
		exists = ITA
		exists = JAP
		has_global_flag = tripartite_pact
	}

	trigger = {
		GER = { faction = axis }
		ITA = { faction = axis }
		JAP = { faction = axis }
	}
	
	ruling_party_support = 0.025
	research_efficiency = 0.05
	espionage_bonus = 0.05
	global_supplies = 0.05
	icon = 12
}
## Lapland War
lapland_war = {

	potential = {
		tag = FIN
	}
	
	trigger = {
		GER = { war_with = FIN }
		or = {
			month = 11
			not = {
				month = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	org_regain = 0.1
	reinforcement_bonus = 0.15
	land_organisation = 0.05
	
	icon = 10
}
## General Winter
general_winter = {

	potential = {
		not =  {has_global_flag = NO_MODIFIERS }
		tag = SOV
		has_country_modifier = patriotic_war
	}
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		war_with = GER
		GER = {
			or = {
				controls = 1534
				controls = 2223
				controls = 1991
				controls = 3175
				controls = 1535
				controls = 1182
				controls = 1102
				controls = 909
				controls = 782
			}
		}
		or = {
			month = 11
			not = {
				month = 3
			}
		}
	}
	
	org_regain = 0.25
	territorial_pride = 0.05
	#defence_modifier = 0.6
	#offence_modifier = 0.2
	reinforcement_bonus = 0.5
	
	icon = 8
}

# desperate_defence

	potential = {
		not =  {has_global_flag = NO_MODIFIERS }
		tag = CHI
		JAP = { ai = yes }	
	}
	
	trigger = {
		not = { controls = 4685 }
		not = { controls = 5020 }
		not = { controls = 5182 }
		not = { controls = 5341 }
		not = { controls = 7139 }
		war_with = JAP
	}
	
	#territorial_pride = 0.05
	org_regain = 0.025
	land_organisation = -0.25
	global_leadership_modifier = -0.3
	
	icon = 5
}

soviet_china_aid_sov = {

	potential = {
		tag = SOV
		has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid
		NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid_early }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid_cancel }
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid
	}
	
	global_leadership = -1
	global_money = -0.15
	global_supplies = -0.15
	
	icon = 13
}

soviet_china_aid_chi = {

	potential = {
		tag = CHI
		has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid
		SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid_early }}
		SOV = { NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid_cancel } }
	}
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_china_aid
	}
	
	global_leadership = 1
	unit_start_experience = 10
	global_money = 0.10
	global_supplies = 0.15
	air_organisation = 0.05
	
	icon = 13
}
######### MarneMod - Pacific Island Hopping Campaign ###########
# Island Hopping Bonus 1 - for 8 islands captured and held
island_effect_1 = {

	potential = {
		or = {
			tag = USA
			tag = JAP
		}
		this = { check_variable = { which = "islandsHopped" value = 8 } }
		not = { this = { check_variable = { which = "islandsHopped" value = 9 } } }
		USA = { war_with = JAP	}
	}

	trigger = {
		or = {
			tag = USA
			tag = JAP
		}
	}
	
	global_manpower_modifier = 0.01
	national_unity = 0.01
	global_ic = 0.01
	dissent = -0.01
	supply_throughput = 0.02
	
	icon = 24
}

	potential = {
		war_with = SOV
		tag = GER
		has_country_flag = bahnhof_riga
		not = { 
			and = { has_country_flag = bahnhof_talinn 	
				906 = { controller = { faction = axis } }	
				1178 = { controller = { faction = axis } }
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		1178 = {
			controller = { faction = axis }
		}
	}

	icon = 30 
}

########## SMALL SHIPYARDS COUNT #######################################################

triggered_mod_small_shipyard_core_1 = { 
	potential = {
		check_variable = { which = "small_ship_shipyard_count" value = 1 }
		not = { check_variable = { which = "small_ship_shipyard_count" value = 2 } }
	}
	trigger = {
		check_variable = { which = "small_ship_shipyard_count" value = 1 }
		not = { check_variable = { which = "small_ship_shipyard_count" value = 2 } }
	}

	icon = 50
}

		not = { check_variable = { which = "rail_terminous_count" value = 99 } }
	}
	trigger = {

		not = { check_variable = { which = "rail_terminous_count" value = 99 } }
	}
	#naval_build_speed = -0.24

}
